<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:повесть.html>повести</a> (2118)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вести.html>вести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повесть.html>повести́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">povestí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вести.html>вести́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lead, to conduct, to direct, to drive</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повесть.html>повести́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">povestí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поводить.html>поводи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to move
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:повесть.html>повести</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бровь.html>бровя́ми</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>povesti</b> brovjámi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to raise one's brows; lift one's eyebrows</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бровь.html>бро́вью</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:ухо.html>у́хом</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:повести.html>повёл</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on i bróvʹju/úxom ne <b>povjól</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation"> he did not turn a hair; he did not bat an eyelid</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повесть.html>по́вести</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">póvesti</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> <abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">genitive singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повесть.html>по́весть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">póvestʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ве<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>сти́</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 7b/b.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:вести.html>вести</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:поводить.html>поводи́ть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-вес-</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ти</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повесть.html>повести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">povestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-сь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повестись.html>повести́сь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">povestísʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to become the custom
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уж.html>уж</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:повестись.html>повело́сь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">už tak <b>povelósʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">such is the custom</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make friends <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">with</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>ке́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:повестись.html>поведёшься</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>того́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:набраться.html>наберёшься</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s kem povedjóšʹsja, ot tovó i naberjóšʹsja</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">he who lies down with dogs, gets up with fleas</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">with whom you <b>make friends</b>, from him you will gain</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повесть.html>повести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">povestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ве<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>сти́сь</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 7b/b.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:вестись.html>вести́сь</a>, поводиться.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-вес-</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ти</b>; постфикс: <b>-сь</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ве́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>шен<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p>Страдательное <a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>прича́стие</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:прошедший.html>проше́дшего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. ***повеять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:повеять.html>пове́ять</a> (17002)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:веять.html>ве́ять</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">véjatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повеять.html>пове́ять</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">povéjatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to begin to blow
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:повеять.html>пове́яло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:прохлада.html>прохла́дой</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>povéjalo</b> proxládoj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">there came a breath of cool air; the air grew fresher</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be in the air, to be able to be sensed
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:повеять.html>пове́яло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:отчужденность.html>отчуждённостью</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ot nevó <b>povéjalo</b> otčuždjónnostʹju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">one could sense some estrangement in him</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:повзрослевший.html>повзросле́вший</a> (14119)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повзрослевший.html>повзросле́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">povzroslévšij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past active perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повзрослеть.html>повзросле́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">povzroslétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:повзрослевший.html>повзросле́вший</a></b>

***повидать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:повидать.html>повида́ть</a> (7121)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:видать.html>вида́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vidátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повидать.html>повида́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">povidátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:видать.html>вида́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to see, to get to see
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:многое.html>мно́гое</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:повидать.html>повида́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>своём</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:век.html>веку́</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On mnógoje <b>povidál</b> na svojóm vekú.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He got to see a lot in his life.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to visit
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:очень.html>о́чень</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:устать.html>уста́ли</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:зато.html>зато́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:повидать.html>повида́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>друзе́й</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">My óčenʹ ustáli, no zató <b>povidáli</b> druzéj.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">We got very tired but (for all that) we visited (our) friends.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***повидло.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:повидло.html>пови́дло</a> (25118)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">powidło</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повидло.html>пови́дло</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">povídlo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повидло.html>пови́дла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повидло.html>пови́дла</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повидло.html>пови́дл</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>jam, marmalade, fruit butter, fruit paste</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:повисать.html>повиса́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:повиснуть.html>пови́снуть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-вис-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
